{"answers": ["An elevator with a counterbalance"], "model_answer": "Based on the provided documents, a real-world application of an Atwood machine is an elevator with a counterbalance. {"answers": ["diastema (plural diastemata)", "diastema"], "model_answer": "Based on the provided documents, the answer to the question is \"diastema\". A diastema is a space or gap between two teeth, and it is commonly found between the incisors and molars in many species of mammals. In the context of human teeth, a diastema can occur between the front teeth, and it is often caused by an imbalance in the relationship between the jaw and the size of the teeth."}

{"answers": ["balance sheet", "The balance sheet"], "model_answer": "Based on the provided documents, the answer is the Balance Sheet. The Balance Sheet is the financial statement that shows a firm's assets, liabilities, and equity (capital) at a set point in time, usually the end of the fiscal year reported on the accompanying income statement. The total assets always equal the total combined liabilities and equity in dollar amount, demonstrating the basic accounting equation - Assets = Liabilities + Equity."}
